  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer16509824639206262300">Sweet tea, corn bread, and soup beans—everyday fare for eight-year-old Alix French, the precocious darling of a respected southern family. But nothing was ordinary about the day she met ten-year-old Nick Anderson, a boy from the wrong side of town.   <span id="freeText16509824639206262300" style="display:none">Sweet tea, corn bread, and soup beans—everyday fare for eight-year-old Alix French, the precocious darling of a respected southern family. But nothing was ordinary about the day she met ten-year-old Nick Anderson, a boy from the wrong side of town. Armed with only a tin of bee balm and steely determination, Alix treats the raw evidence of a recent beating that mars his back, an act that changes both of their lives forever.<br /><br />Through childhood disasters and teenage woes they cling together as friendship turns to love. The future looks rosy until the fateful night when Frank Anderson, Nick's abusive father, is shot to death in his filthy trailer.<br /><br />Suddenly, Nick is gone—leaving Alix alone, confused and pregnant. For the next fifteen years she wrestles with the pain of Nick's abandonment, a bad marriage, her family and friends. But finally, she's starting to get her life back together. Her divorce is almost final, her business is booming, and she's content if not happy—until the day she looks up and sees Nick standing across the counter. He's back…and he's not alone.<br /><br />Once again Alix is plunged into turmoil and pain as Nick tries to win her love, something she resists with all her strength. Only one thing might break the protective wall she's built around her emotions—the truth about Frank Anderson's death. But when that truth comes out and those walls crumble, neither Alix nor Nick is prepared for the emotional explosion that could destroy as well as heal.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16509824639206262300" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/184123-what-year-is-this-book-set-in-there-are">What year is this book set in? There are few contextual clues. At age 8, she&#39;s reading Dune, which was first published in 1965...of course it was republished many times since then. The Beatles and Rolling Stones were referenced in the beginning of the book, suggesting 1960s-1970s. Computers and video games are mentioned at the end when the main characters were in their 30s.....any ideas?</a>
</div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257873893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5261614856522272495">5.5 stars<br/><br/><i> <b> "You're the only one I've ever wanted, Alix, the only one I'll ever want. That's a promise." </b></i> <br/><br/>Oh WOW !!! What a BEAUTIFUL, AMAZING book!! Love! love! love!!<br/><br/>I'm a mess - it was an intense, utterly riveting book that I literally <i> could not </i> put down, that kept my heart racing, kept me near tears for a good chunk of it, that had me hanging off of every word that I read, and the story just ripped my heart out but yet still had a very sweet ending.<br/><br/>The writing was beautiful and flowed effor</span>
  <span id="freeText5261614856522272495" style="display:none">5.5 stars<br><br><i> <b> "You're the only one I've ever wanted, Alix, the only one I'll ever want. That's a promise." </b></i> <br><br>Oh WOW !!! What a BEAUTIFUL, AMAZING book!! Love! love! love!!<br><br>I'm a mess - it was an intense, utterly riveting book that I literally <i> could not </i> put down, that kept my heart racing, kept me near tears for a good chunk of it, that had me hanging off of every word that I read, and the story just ripped my heart out but yet still had a very sweet ending.<br><br>The writing was beautiful and flowed effortlessly, the characters were vivid, and the story was gripping and sucked you right in from the start.<br><br>If you are looking for a captivating, bittersweet, emotional read with a happy ending, this is it!<br><br>I started reading this book around midnight after a whole day of traveling expecting to just read for an hour and put it down. Boy was I wrong! I read straight through the night and finished the book around 6am when the sun came up!! I just couldn't tear myself away from it!<br><br>The first half of the book starts out in a small Southern town where Alix, an 8 year-old girl from a very well-respected family who reaches out to help Nick, the 10-year old son of a dead-beat drunk who owns the local salvage yard. She befriends him and over the years, her family shelters him as he and Alix grow closer and closer. Even from a young age, they have a connection that is just so beautiful and powerful.<br><br><i> "...while I was vowing to save Nick, he had taken on the job of being my protector and staunchest defender." </i><br><br>As they grow up, it becomes impossible for them to deny the love they've always had for each other.<br><br><i> "There was only one boy I wanted, and I lived for the times when I could be alone with him. It was simple. When I was with Nick, I was happy. When I wasn't, I was restless and miserable." </i><br><br>But when tragedy outside of their control strikes, Nick is forced to leave town. The second half of the book occurs 15 years later when Nick returns home and tries with everything he's got to put their relationship back together.<br><br>This book got me so into it, that when I read these words, <i> "Then, fifteen years after he left, Nick came home." </i> , I just felt my heart clenched right up and tears literally just started falling from my cheeks. I just needed things to be made right again so badly.<br><br><i> <b> "Do you want to know the real reason I came back, Alix? It was because of you. You're my roots. Wherever you are would be home to me...I've never stopped loving you. I won't give up that easily." </b></i> <br><br>There is a huge twist to the story with secrets that comes out explaining the true reason why he had to leave that had me almost hyperventilating and clutching at my heart.<br><br>This story is about powerful love, loss and betrayal, family, second chances, secrets that test the strength of family and relationship bonds, overcoming prejudices, but most importantly its about a very beautiful and sweet love story that start when Alix and Nick were young and never lets go throughout all the years of hardship.<br><br>The book was told from Alix's perspective - almost as if she were retelling it from the end. But I loved how, especially in the first part of the book when she is a child, she explains it through the eyes of child while still giving insight on the side from her adult, mature self.<br><br>I just totally fell in love with Nick. He's was exactly my kind of hero - first he was totally HOT, but what really melted my heart was how protective he was. I just love that quality in a man. And he was just such a GOOD guy - so respectful, always trying to do the right thing, and he was just completely, utterly swoony. I'm smiling as I write this just thinking about him.<br><br>But that isn't to say that he (or Alix) was perfect - they made their fair share of mistakes but the mistakes were understandable... I didn't always agree with what they did, but I could totally understand why they did it. But the strength of their love for each other won out in the end.<br><br>The intensity of Nick and Alix's love took my breath away at times and while there are a fair number of sex scenes, they are not portrayed very graphically. They are more focused on descriptions of emotions rather than acts.<br><br>I think fans of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11784281.Take_This_Regret" title="Take This Regret by A.L. Jackson" rel="nofollow noopener">Take This Regret</a> will really enjoy this book, and vice versa.<br><br>This book is going on my favorites shelf! Absolutely LOVED it!! A <b> must-read!! </b><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366708i/719010._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5261614856522272495" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/331412459" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=weepy">weepy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer331412459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11413823604690066926"><b>BREATHTAKING!</b><br/><br/>Books like <i>The Sweet Gum Tree</i> are why I love to read. Filled with beauty, symbolism, heartache, forgiveness, redemption, and an undying love all around—this ultimate love story turned out to be one of the greatest books I've ever read!<br/><br/>Since the synopsis for this book is generous and intriguing enough, I don't feel a summation of the story here is necessary. But I will say that each and and every one of these characters had been broken and slowly redeemed and held a special place in </span>
  <span id="freeText11413823604690066926" style="display:none"><b>BREATHTAKING!</b><br><br>Books like <i>The Sweet Gum Tree</i> are why I love to read. Filled with beauty, symbolism, heartache, forgiveness, redemption, and an undying love all around—this ultimate love story turned out to be one of the greatest books I've ever read!<br><br>Since the synopsis for this book is generous and intriguing enough, I don't feel a summation of the story here is necessary. But I will say that each and and every one of these characters had been broken and slowly redeemed and held a special place in my heart throughout this extraordinary book.  I enjoyed  being present during Nick and Alix's transition from childhood to adulthood. It was such an incredible way to build a palpable connection and understanding for the characters. <br><br>I love reading books with references to the finer things in life. I was mesmerized by the descriptions of nature and its comparison to humanity. Nick was Alix's "sweet gum tree", and his love stood deeply rooted in Alix's life no matter how the storms threatened to rip them apart. <br><br>Although this story was heartbreaking throughout, it didn't remain tragic or leave me feeling depleted. The  heartache actually intensified its sweetness instead of reducing it. What I loved most about this story was its example that true love is strong enough to forgive and withstand any element that threatens to break it. Most of the time, the choices we make in life deeply affect our future...but some of life's downfalls are completely out of our hands. We have to allow ourselves the time to grieve in order to properly heal so we can, eventually, be able to live again. <br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Moderate/Steamy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Childhood to adulthood romance. Sweet, angsty, and emotional. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Damaged, lovable and very well-fleshed out.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Focused on redemption, forgiveness, and healing. Slight twist.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Brilliant and cultured. Engrossing storytelling. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine <br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None/Standalone <br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_399696000" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/399696000" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/399696000?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer399696000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13789822557130859501"><b>5 Beautiful Stars! </b><br/><br/>If you are like me, and have just had this book sitting on your e-reader for months and haven’t gotten around to it, do yourself a favor and bump it to the top of your TBR list! Such an amazing, beautiful, sweet, and at times- heartbreaking story.<br/><br/>Alix and Nick (as adults)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/3764a579-38f4-4479-8390-fa15e752fe09_zps6df649dd.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749774.jpg' alt=' photo 3764a579-38f4-4479-8390-fa15e752fe09_zps6df649dd.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/14bee0ba-e8bf-4fa7-b207-f31a9f2db51f_zps81d7b643.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749775._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 14bee0ba-e8bf-4fa7-b207-f31a9f2db51f_zps81d7b643.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Alix French and Nick Anderson both grew up in the same small town. They meet when Alix is 8 and Nick is 10. Alix comes from a good family. She lives with her grandfather ‘Judge’, her mama and her two a</span>
  <span id="freeText13789822557130859501" style="display:none"><b>5 Beautiful Stars! </b><br><br>If you are like me, and have just had this book sitting on your e-reader for months and haven’t gotten around to it, do yourself a favor and bump it to the top of your TBR list! Such an amazing, beautiful, sweet, and at times- heartbreaking story.<br><br>Alix and Nick (as adults)<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/3764a579-38f4-4479-8390-fa15e752fe09_zps6df649dd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749774.jpg" alt=" photo 3764a579-38f4-4479-8390-fa15e752fe09_zps6df649dd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/14bee0ba-e8bf-4fa7-b207-f31a9f2db51f_zps81d7b643.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749775._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 14bee0ba-e8bf-4fa7-b207-f31a9f2db51f_zps81d7b643.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alix French and Nick Anderson both grew up in the same small town. They meet when Alix is 8 and Nick is 10. Alix comes from a good family. She lives with her grandfather ‘Judge’, her mama and her two aunts. Nick doesn’t have the same home life. He lives with his drunk father, who runs the junkyard and is abusive to him. He doesn’t have too many friends, and Alix decides to befriend him. A beautiful friendship between the two of them begins. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/add0ad41-dfd8-4403-bcd4-1a72d82b29c6_zpsb73f3f38.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749776.jpg" alt=" photo add0ad41-dfd8-4403-bcd4-1a72d82b29c6_zpsb73f3f38.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nick and Alix grow up together. Nick becomes part of the family to the other French’s. He often stays in the spare room of their barn when his dad is particularly nasty. As they grow up and get older, the feelings the two of them have start to go past friendship. They develop real feelings for one another. Nick never feels good enough for Alix. It’s a hurdle for their relationship.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ec198bb3-fee9-42dd-8f86-df46ad563a04_zps75a3acb6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749777.jpg" alt=" photo ec198bb3-fee9-42dd-8f86-df46ad563a04_zps75a3acb6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nick and Alix start to fall in love. They date ‘secretly’. Alix is technically seeing a guy who her mama wants her with, but she doesn’t love Hugh. She only cares about him like a friend. Nick’s the only man she has ever wanted. She wants to break up with Hugh, but things are complicated with her and Nick.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/SweetGumTree-Drivein_zpsbbb003cd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749778.jpg" alt=" photo SweetGumTree-Drivein_zpsbbb003cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Nick has a neighbor named Lindsey he is particularly close to. He has been like a big brother to her, and she needs his help. That is why Nick and Alix’s relationship has to be a secret. This goes on for months. Finally, Alix makes Nick chose. He of course, chooses her.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f5af6f35-8411-4d1f-8d68-3b5db9276399_zps373a5a68.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749779.jpg" alt=" photo f5af6f35-8411-4d1f-8d68-3b5db9276399_zps373a5a68.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The morning they are going to come clean with her family about their relationship, she finds out something shocking. Nick’s father Frank has been murdered. And Nick is in jail. It looks as though it was self defense, so they give Nick a choice to leave town and join the Army. He takes it. This devastates Alix. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/41fcb489-ce7a-4ae9-84e4-6cb9bd195e3a_zpsb4eb0179.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749780.jpg" alt=" photo 41fcb489-ce7a-4ae9-84e4-6cb9bd195e3a_zpsb4eb0179.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alix learns that<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You can’t turn love on and off like a light switch, no matter how hard you try.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>Many heartbreaking things happen from here...<br>Alix finds herself <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[pregnant with Nick’s baby. She is only 18 and getting ready to graduate high school. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Hugh, the guy she has been seeing finds out all about Nick and wants to marry her anyway. Because of the circumstances, and Nick telling her he’s never coming back and to move on- she agrees. <br><br>Something devastating happens to Alix that year. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Her baby, Katie, dies of SIDS at 6 months old. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> She never gets past it. She is in a loveless marriage for 15 years before she decides enough is enough and files for divorce. She works hard at her company, her job is her life. Her family and friends are worried.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You walk and talk and breathe and eat, you work and sleep, but you aren’t alive anymore.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Right before her divorce is final, she see’s him. Nick Anderson is back in town. He brings her back to life, but not in the way you imagine. She blames Nick, hates him for what he did. Especially now that he has brought a son with him. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ A son that would be the same age as her daughter and looks a lot like Katie <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Its too much for Alix.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I do not love Nick. I hate him.” <br>“No, you only think you do. Alix, the opposite of love isn’t hate, it’s indifference. And you couldn’t be indifferent to him if your life depended on it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Nick can’t explain everything quite yet, but he tries to get through to Alix. He loves her, he’s never stopped loving her and he wants to be with her.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Do you want to know the real reason I came back, Alix? It was because of you. You’re my roots. Wherever you are would be home to me.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>It takes a lot of convincing for Alix to realize this, but once she hears the truth, will she ever be able to forgive Nick? I guessed part of the big twist early on... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I knew Nick would NEVER cheat on Alix. I had a feeling the baby was Franks. I wasn’t sure about who killed him, but it didnt’ surprise me that it was Lindsay. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I swear, I’ll never leave you again.” he whispered<br>“It wouldn’t do you any good if you did,” I said. “Because the next time, I’d come after you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>This a solid 5 star read for me, one of my new favorite ya books! Nick and Alix’s journey is sweet and beautiful, but it is also heartbreaking and tragic. Those two went through so much, but through it all, they still had an unbreakable bond. The writing was beautiful, and the ending will make your heart happy!!! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/38d86919-01e8-4084-8794-9c3d17515de9_zpsea3e7d94.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749781.jpg" alt=" photo 38d86919-01e8-4084-8794-9c3d17515de9_zpsea3e7d94.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5532343251753046757"><b><br/><i><blockquote>He brushed my hair back. “You’re the only one I’ve ever wanted, Alix, the only one I’ll ever want. That’s a promise.”</blockquote>
<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381490988ra/4939123.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>“God, I can’t lose you again.” His whisper was harsh, filled with pain. “Not now, when I’ve waited so long to hold you. I think it would kill me. But I’m so damn scared you’ll hate me when you find out the truth.”</blockquote></i><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>This was both heartbreaking and sweet <3<br/>Amazing romance that spans decades, from childhood sweethearts to adult intense love.<br/><3<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>The story<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381492870ra/4940782.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote><i>“I didn’t want to stop. It scared</i></blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText5532343251753046757" style="display:none"><b><br><i><blockquote>He brushed my hair back. “You’re the only one I’ve ever wanted, Alix, the only one I’ll ever want. That’s a promise.”</blockquote>
<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381490988ra/4939123.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>“God, I can’t lose you again.” His whisper was harsh, filled with pain. “Not now, when I’ve waited so long to hold you. I think it would kill me. But I’m so damn scared you’ll hate me when you find out the truth.”</blockquote></i><br><br><br><br><br>This was both heartbreaking and sweet &lt;3<br>Amazing romance that spans decades, from childhood sweethearts to adult intense love.<br>&lt;3<br><br><br><br><br>The story<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381492870ra/4940782.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote><i>“I didn’t want to stop. It scared me. You’re the best thing that’s ever happened to me, Alix. I’m not going to let anything hurt you, not even me. I figured I had to stay away from you for your own good.”</i></blockquote></b><br><br><br>Alix and Nick meet while they are children and form an instant friendship.<br>As the years go by, they grow up and fall in love &lt;3<br>It isn't all sunshine and roses because Nick has an abusive father who's making his life hell, and the only good thing Nick has is Alix and her family.<br>A horrible thing happens that drives them apart and makes Alix hate him:(<br><br><br><br><br><b>Alix and Nick<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381492870ra/4940783.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote><i>“I thought I’d lost you,” he murmured. “I’ve never been so afraid in my life. I felt hollow, like part of me had been ripped out.” His shaking finally eased to periodic spasms. “I swear, Alix, someday I’ll make you proud to be seen with me.”</i></blockquote></b><br><br><br>Life was never easy on those two.<br>Not when they were kids, not as teens and certainly not when they are adults.<br>Nick's father was always there to make his life miserable and I felt sorry for Nick from the start :(<br>He grew up to be an amazing man and I love him like crazy &lt;3<br>Alix... I can't say that I loved her, she was OK and she got on my nerves in the second part of the book, really got on my nerves :D<br>But as a couple, I loved them and their heartbreaking romance &lt;3<br><br><br><br><br><b>Overall<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434014ra/873787.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>What I liked:</b><br><br>I enjoyed the book as a whole, I couldn't stop reading! It was emotionally intense, especially when it hit 50%!<br>The romance was great even though pretty much sad all the time, but surprisingly, it didn't bother me! It was still sweet, especially at the end.<br>I looooved Nick &lt;3 OMG he is amazing &lt;3<br><br><b>What I didn't like:</b><br><br>The long intro into the real story.<br>I am not a fan of this, especially when it's to do with their pasts and too much detail.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[50% of the book in their childhood/teens is way too long for my taste. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Having said that, the childhood part was interesting, so as the teen years, I can't say I hated reading it cause I loved those two together, I just wish it was SHORTER!<br><br>The melodrama at the end.<br>I am not a melodrama fan either and the ending was a bit weird for me, especially the epilogue. I guess I wanted something more and more intense than what I got.<br>I did like the ending overall because of what happened between them, again, I just wish it wasn't so melodramatic.<br><br><br><br><b>Now I know it seems like I complained a lot, but I only disliked those two things, while I loved the book itself. <br>Weird but there you go, I even loved the angsty part if you can believe it :DDD<br><br>So for everyone who loves a heartbreaking romance with a HEA, grab this one, you won't regret it :)<br></b><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_388327079" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/388327079" />
    <a title="Zeek" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek"><img alt="Zeek" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339154824p2/2478293.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/388327079?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zeek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zeek" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek">Zeek</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer388327079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9311022598830267411">The Sweet Gum Tree started out brilliantly. Expertly setting the scene of smalltown livin in the deep south, I was hooked. Even more so when little Alix French befriends a boy from the wrong side of the tracks by introducing him to her favorite books. They become a fierce unit and it’s easy to see they are destined soul mates. I loved Nick and Alix. Together. Apart? Not so much, because they were stupid. Period. When things begin to happen to keep them apart, the book fell apart for me too. <br/><br/>Here</span>
  <span id="freeText9311022598830267411" style="display:none">The Sweet Gum Tree started out brilliantly. Expertly setting the scene of smalltown livin in the deep south, I was hooked. Even more so when little Alix French befriends a boy from the wrong side of the tracks by introducing him to her favorite books. They become a fierce unit and it’s easy to see they are destined soul mates. I loved Nick and Alix. Together. Apart? Not so much, because they were stupid. Period. When things begin to happen to keep them apart, the book fell apart for me too. <br /><br />Here we go again, "The Big Misunderstanding" plot device. I'm okay with it, truly I am- if the reason that keeps them apart doesnt do so beyond reasonable explanation. With The Sweet Gum Tree? Not so much.<br /><br />See the secret that Nick holds is supposed to be something deep and mysterious, kept close to the his vest. But it was obvious to me from the get go. Which seriously ticked me off- because it screamed- “C’mon- it's gotta something more than <i>that</i>!?”, which made me want to scream at the heroine, "YOU IDIOT! Can't you see what he's doing?!". <br /><br />To make it worse, he keeps perpetuating the misunderstanding BY NOT TELLING HER THE TRUTH. bbbluuurghhh<br /><br />Add that to me being already irritated with Alix for clinging to her misplaced hatred toward the man she supposedly once loved to her very soul and I was over my first blush of excitement fairly quickly. (She also came off pretty dang blind by not seeing what was so patently obvious not only with Nick and the woman she thought he was in love with behind her back, but also with her best friend.) <br /><br />There's nothing I hate more then the feel of manufactured drama. Either make it plausible or go over the top. This just ticked me off. <br /><br />Oh and one more thing- the author’s heavy handed foreshadowing- no wait, fore<i>warning</i> because there was no shadowing about it. She outright <i>said</i> they were doomed. At the end of every chapter. <br /><br />Though I kept reading, I was done about 40% in.<br /><br />Generous 2 pts- 1 for keeping me reading and 1 for the magnificent setting and characters. Everything else? Amateur.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9311022598830267411" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_474518810" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/474518810" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474518810?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=loved-you-since-childhood">loved-you-since-childhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=young-adult-new-adult">young-adult-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=pissed-me-the-fuck-off">pissed-me-the-fuck-off</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer474518810&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474518810" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3765743826738006602"><i>Re-read 11/23/14...Still powerful...still pissed off...</i><br/><br/><b>5 Pissed Me the F&$k Off Stars</b><br/><br/>This book actually made me create a whole new shelf: my pissed me the fuck off shelf. And yet, I'm giving it 5 stars. Believe me, I am as confused as you. I knew immediately after reading this that I was either gonna rate this 1 star or 5 stars, because I had a love/hate relationship going on with this thing. <br/><br/>The whole time I'm reading this. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395933758ra/9064638.gif' width='500' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And yet, I couldn't put the damn thing down. I stayed up late and am no</span>
  <span id="freeText3765743826738006602" style="display:none"><i>Re-read 11/23/14...Still powerful...still pissed off...</i><br><br><b>5 Pissed Me the F&amp;$k Off Stars</b><br><br>This book actually made me create a whole new shelf: my pissed me the fuck off shelf. And yet, I'm giving it 5 stars. Believe me, I am as confused as you. I knew immediately after reading this that I was either gonna rate this 1 star or 5 stars, because I had a love/hate relationship going on with this thing. <br><br>The whole time I'm reading this. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395933758ra/9064638.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And yet, I couldn't put the damn thing down. I stayed up late and am now sleep deprived. <br><br>Always the sign of a winner. Now excuse me while I rant. <br><br>This was one of those story lines that I love: the whole "we fall in love as children" that sucks me in my every time. I already knew I love that shtick; however, what I did NOT realize until I read this book is that I loathe the "I am going to be a martyr and make myself and everyone around me miserable as a result" shtick. LOATHE it. <br><br>I get it. You wanna be all sacrificial for the ones you love. I can respect that. But we gotta draw the line somewhere, damn it. <br><br>Nick? Not my favorite. <br><br>I get that he wanted to help Lindsey (fuck that bitch by the way). But when you sacrifice your entire life because someone else refuses to take responsibility for their's?<br><br>Hell to the no. <br><br>He didn't need to take the fall for Lindsey. If they had just been honest and told the truth about the rape, it wouldn't have been any worse for Lindsey. She still would have been pregnant and ended up 5150 (that's cop code for "hold pending crazy", a la Britney Spears). <br><br>In fact, maybe being HONEST about what happened might have been <i>healing</i> for her. But no, Nick had to ruin his life, Alix's life, Hugh's life, Jenna's life...you get the idea.<br><br>In my opinion, Nick continuously chose to be a martyr for Lindsey instead of being a man for Alix. He kept choosing Lindsey.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416851824ra/12082172.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I know, I know...I should have sympathy for Lindsey. <br><br>But I don't. <br><br>Call me cold and callous (because I am), but I just don't have patience for people who refuse to help themselves out. I get that she had a shitty, neglected childhood. But cry me a river, lots of fucking people have. Using your childhood to make excuses for shitty behavior for <b>the rest of your life</b> makes about as much sense to me as this does:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416851824ra/12082173.gif" width="340" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Because she refused to give herself an assist and leave town or - I don't know - CALL THE POLICE, she was basically the catalyst for the ruination of many lives, not just her own. It annoyed the shit out of me and I have no patience for it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416851824ra/12082174.gif" width="280" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall though, this book sucked me in, it was well written, it had solid, defined characters and I loved the reminiscent Southern vibe weaved throughout. <br><br>And it takes talent to make a reader love and hate an entire book at the same time.<br> <br>Well done, Ms. Allred!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3765743826738006602" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_323250943" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/323250943" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/323250943?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=irresistable-hot-guys">irresistable-hot-guys</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer323250943" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15982643771763621132">OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG *deep breaths*<br/>Holy shit....that was THE BEST EFFING BOOK I've EVER read....hands down!!!! TWENTY stars. Omg I have a headache and my eyes are sore from the fifty million full on sobs I did. <br/><br/>I shall have a full review soon....<br/><br/>BEFORE I GO INTO THIS REVIEW.....EVERYONE NEEDS TO READ THIS BOOK! EVERYONE! READ THIS BOOK! I MEAN IT! READ. THIS. BOOK. Thank you!<br/><br/><br/>If I could give this book EVERY star in the world, I certianly would. My emotions are still raw after finishing thi</span>
  <span id="freeText15982643771763621132" style="display:none">OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG *deep breaths*<br />Holy shit....that was THE BEST EFFING BOOK I've EVER read....hands down!!!! TWENTY stars. Omg I have a headache and my eyes are sore from the fifty million full on sobs I did. <br /><br />I shall have a full review soon....<br /><br />BEFORE I GO INTO THIS REVIEW.....EVERYONE NEEDS TO READ THIS BOOK! EVERYONE! READ THIS BOOK! I MEAN IT! READ. THIS. BOOK. Thank you!<br /><br /><br />If I could give this book EVERY star in the world, I certianly would. My emotions are still raw after finishing this book at 5 this morning. So a decent review is not feasible right now. But make no mistake, this book is UNFORGETTABLE, EPIC, GUT WRENCHINGLY BEAUTIFUL novel I've EVER read and I can't think straight for the life of me. But I will have a long throrough review when I can function correctly. <br /><br />Oh Lord, where do I begin?? This book is still so fresh on my mind that I could see every bit of the story through my eyes. It was simply, simply amazing, wonderful, unforgettable. Oh my God, I just love this book so damn much. I want to read it all over again just to be with the characters once again! <br /><br />I am recommending this book to EVERYONE! It is truly my absolute FAVORITE book of ALL TIME. And though I may say quite often how a book is my favorite blah blah blah....nope....not like this one is! This book and Take This Regret are my TWO favorite books EVER! They are so unique and heartbreaking and gutwrenching and insides twisting....GAH! I'm getting emotional all over again. Dammit! <br /><br />*deep breaths*<br /><br />So first of all, I didn't realize this book is 7 years old. I'll admit when I first saw this book on GR, I was a little deterred from reading it because the cover did look kind of old school. I guess the cover doesn't attract many people. But honestly, once you read it, you totally understand what the cover symbolizes which okay it's not the greatest cover but it makes a Hell of alot more sense! I just hope Katherine will update it and make it more eye catching to get more people to read it because IT DESERVES MORE RECOGNITION. But to me, I do love it now that I know what the book is about. So, okay the cover....check.<br /><br />Ummm, I normally know what I want to cover on my reviews but I am so scatterbrained with this book that I have no idea how to really get into the review itself. This book simply took my breath away. Thanks to Erin, my greatest and wonderful ally and sidekick....she introduced me to the most poetic, captivating, heartbreaking, sweet and fun book I've EVER read! I read her review and saw her updates and it became more and more intriguing....and she was recommending this book like crazy. So as I saw more people reading it and having the same reaction I figured it was time to jump on this book and see what the hype was about.<br /><br />HOLY SHITBALLS! HOLY SHITBALLS! MY God. Holy Hell. Dammit.<br /><br />When I started this I was instantly swept away by not only the characters but the descriptions. They were so vivid that I could picture every bit of this amazing place that Katherine painted for us. It was like seeing it firsthand. I felt like I was inside the story and watching it, feeling all the emotions the characters felt. Not one character did I end up not liking and for the life of me, it started out that way. But by the end, I called them all my family. My friends. I cried when I finished because not only is the ending bittersweet, but I didn't want to leave them. Oh my God, I loved them so much! I've read plenty of contemporary romance novels, but by far this is the BEST! <br /><br />The Sweet Gum Tree takes place within 26 years. Alix, the town's rich kid and Nick, son of start as friends at the age of 8 and 10. Alix(8) befriends Nick(10), saving him from his horrible life. His father is a real asshole and he's abbusive and I wanted to beat the fuck out of him for everything he did. Holy shit, that man is the epitome of a sick fuck! And when you read this, you'll understand my hatred for him. So Nick being scared and worried about what others think, since he is the son of a drunk and white trash, living in a salvage junk yard....he's very skittish. He loves to read but his father thinks reading is a waste of time, but yet he spends all his time drunk off his ass instead of being a father to his son. Slowly, Nick lets his guard down and he and Alix get closer. Their friendship is absolutely captivating and beautiful. He becomes a protector of her, and as they get older and she starts asking him hilarious questions about babies and marriage, I can't help but laugh and feel so much love for them. Alix is so smart and she's very inquisitive, leaving Nick to answer odd questions. But he doesn't mind. When night when he is so beat up by his dad, Alix puts him up in a room in their barn next to their house and her grandfather who lives with them and happens to be the judge of town, helps him with his wounds. Then he goes to Nick's house and tells his father that is he ever hurts Nick again, he'll be thrown in jail. <br />After that, you don't see him making that mistake....but that doesn't mean he doesn't do some other shit. But still, Nick comes over and sleeps in that room that becomes his own for whenever he wants to get away from his dad, especially after he’s been drinking. He’s made a promise to the Judge that he would, to avoid getting abused again. It works well for Alix and Nick. As their friendship blossoms and gets more intense, you see how much their love for one another is so strong and its beautiful. Though he’s still afraid of what others will say, they don’t tell anyone. As they are in middle school and she goes through changes, so does he. And of course she notices and it’s quite funny. Their banter and conversations between one another is so awesome! Some of his quotes are unforgettable. <br /><br />“You’re not old enough to have a real boyfriend,” he muttered. <br />I stiffened.<br />“If I’m old enough to have babies, then I’m damn well old enough to have a boyfriend,” I ground out. “And just as soon as I decide on who it’s going to be, I’ll let you know.”<br /><br />Once they became a couple, their relationship was so consuming. You were so in love with both of them. He was the perfect gentleman and very gentle with her. It was really neat that they were both virgins so the first time they have sex was hot but also funny because she wasn’t sure if they were doing it right. I couldn’t help but laugh. I loved it though! He never made her do anything she was uncomfortable with which is why it took them awhile to get it on….I kept hoping early on that they would do it already. But Nick was chivalrous and I loved that about him. Oh there was a scene between them….him thrusting her up against his car while making out was HOT HOT HOT! Ahhhhh, he’s one sexy beast!!<br />In the meantime, we meet the Judge, Aunt Darla, Aunt Jane, Jenna (Alix’s best friend), Hugh and many more characters that I will never forget.<br />Once things get good for Nick and Alix, they finally make it a point to tell the family that they are together. But I guess not everything goes your way. Something bad happens, something so life changing your heart starts racing rapidly in your chest and Nick has to leave Alix and his life behind. She is so heartbroken, so beside herself….only to discover something worse-she’s pregnant, with his child and he’s gone. It’s right before graduation and she is dating Hugh, another childhood friend who has liked her since they were kids. Both of their families want them to get married and since she is pregnant and he agrees to father Nick’s child…that’s what they do. Get married.<br />They go through life unhappy; they don’t really love each other. Alix still wants Nick in her life and Hugh starts looking elsewhere. It’s a disaster. They divorce and her mother becomes angry with her and doesn’t talk to her for a while. It’s one thing after another. Alix’s life if so screwed up with another tragedy that hits her square in the gut……..<br />But the day Nick comes back, her life is turned upside down. Questions, many unanswered questions remains in the forefront of her mind. Can they mend what was broken? Can they surpass 15 years of agony and pain they both suffered being apart? Can Alix forgive Nick for leaving her, especially when she needed him most?? Can love really conquer all?<br /><br />“Do you want to know the real reason I came back, Alix?” It was because of you. You’re my roots. Wherever you are would be home to me.”<br /><br />Nick, oh Nick…oh GOD NICK my heart breaks for you all over again, just remembering everything!!! I don’t want to give much else away since I basically told the story(there are some secrets I left out and they are HUGE). I couldn’t help myself….I want to read this book again…NOW! It’s so emotional. They go through the most raw, painful, agonizing, torture, tragic events that I could bear to watch. Just when you think things are going so well for them…..BAM! Another bomb drops and the floor from under you is pulled so forcefully and it’s so unfortunate for them. I love these characters more than most. I loved Nick with all my heart but also I loved Alix a great deal. She faced more tragedy in her life than most in real life and she really became the strongest young lady because of it. I admire her and put her at the top of my FAVORITE HEROINE OF ALL TIME. As much as I love the whole book, the last half was the best. It does have an HEA but don’t be fooled…you need like 10 boxes of tissues and beware; you probably won’t be able to breathe through most of it. But, you HAVE to read this. I encourage ALL ROMANCE LOVERS to read this! You won’t regret it! It will stay with you the rest of your life!<br /> <br />“He always was someone. Because the core of the sweet gum tree never changes. Like Nick, the deep red wood stays true to its nature. Strong, and steady, and pure.” ~Alix~<br /><br />“I promise you this. I’ll love you until the day I die even if I have to live without you. And if it’s fifty years from now, you come home, Nick Anderson. Do you hear me? I’ll be waiting on you.” ~Alix~<br /><br />Those that have read this......we need to form a petition for Katherine to write a novella in Nick's POV. I want to read it sooooooo bad!!!! I want to be in his sexy amazing head and see what he was feeling during this story. We'll all be an emotional wreck for days but I'm already a wreck as it is, so it won't be any different! Ahhh, Nick Anderson...where have you been all my life? </span>
  <a data-text-id="15982643771763621132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_479431244" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/479431244" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/479431244?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9861703-the-sweet-gum-tree">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=emotional-reads">emotional-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=five-plus-stars">five-plus-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=domestic-child-abuse">domestic-child-abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=need-it-in-paperback">need-it-in-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=super-romantic-reads">super-romantic-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=amazing-sexual-tension">amazing-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=virginal-heroine">virginal-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479431244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12016354478233291392"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401130i/778069._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401130i/778070._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Dumbfounded. Gobsmacked. Speechless. Blown away. Overwhelmed... <<< That was me after finishing <i>The Sweet Gum Tree</i> at 3am this morning. <br/><br/>What an absolutely stunning book! I picked it up yesterday afternoon and didn't put it down until the very last page. Absolutely amazing. There aren't enough adjectives for me to express how much I loved this book.<br/><br/>I cried. Quite a lot. You know when you're reading a book and you know you're going to get your heart broken, but you just can't help turn the pages..</span>
  <span id="freeText12016354478233291392" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401130i/778069._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401130i/778070._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dumbfounded. Gobsmacked. Speechless. Blown away. Overwhelmed... &lt;&lt;&lt; That was me after finishing <i>The Sweet Gum Tree</i> at 3am this morning. <br><br>What an absolutely stunning book! I picked it up yesterday afternoon and didn't put it down until the very last page. Absolutely amazing. There aren't enough adjectives for me to express how much I loved this book.<br><br>I cried. Quite a lot. You know when you're reading a book and you know you're going to get your heart broken, but you just can't help turn the pages... and you can feel your soul investing it's every ounce into the characters and their stories. Your emotions slipping through your fingers and out of your control, sucked in by the words on the page... that was this book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm Frank Anderson's son and I live in a junkyard. Who'd want to marry me?"<br>"I'll marry you," I told him decisively. "That way, we can both have kids someday."<br>He grinned, those dimples emerging in a blaze of glory. "Yeah, you probably would."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This was one of those books that makes my other half grumble "You and that bloody Kindle," because I don't react to any conversation, chaos or prodding. <br><br>Nick and Alix's story is so emotional. By 50% I felt like I'd already read an entire book. It was torturous. The love in the book is both palpable and painful. It's an example of innocent people being pulled in so many directions, torn apart and broken down due to circumstances beyond their control... due to their own honor, integrity and goodness, but the poison of others around them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I promise you this. I'll love you until the day I die even if I have to live without you. And if it's fifty years from now, you come home, Nick Anderson. Do you hear me? I'll be waiting on you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Alix falls in love with Nick from an early age, when she decides to 'save' him from his abusive, low-life excuse for a father. The story follows them through childhood and teenage years, until they reach early adulthood... which tears them straight down the middle. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Nick? Have you ever..."<br>"No. I've thought about it, but it never seemed right."<br>"You better wait on me, damn it."<br>"I don't think I have much choice. You're the only one I've ever wanted, Alix, the only one I'll ever want. That's a promise."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Despite his intense love for Alix, Nick is a protector and he can't help but gravitate towards this role. He has dark secrets that he can't share with Alix and tragedy strikes, forcing Nick to leave town and leave Alix. And then all hell breaks loose in part two of this desperate story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm sorry, Nick," I whispered, slipping his pendant from my neck. "I didn't know what else to do."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I thought I was distraught when Nick had to leave... I had no idea what was coming. Oh my goodness, my poor battered, bruised heart. It took a beating. Without giving anything away, all I will say is... Katie. Oh my God, I ugly cried like a goodun! But I always say, I don't having my heart torn out, ripped to pieces and stomped all over, as long as it's put back together and restored by the end of the book. And I can promise that this does have the most satisfying happy-ever-after, ever!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"God, I can't lose you again." His whisper was harsh, filled with pain. "Not now, when I've waited so long to hold you. I think it would kill me. But I'm so damn scared you'll hate me when you find out the truth."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Alix is brilliant. She's great as a child, ballsy and comical, always getting up to mischief and into trouble due to her curious nature. And as she grows up, she becomes an amazing young woman. She faces so much trauma in her life and watching her slip away is awful, but she's strong and resilient and makes you root for her to pull through.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I'd read enough to know that one of the symptoms of grief was a deep anger at the loved one who'd died, anger that impaired your judgement, made you want to scream and curse because they'd left you. But Nick hadn't died, and I didn't realize that I was suffering the symptoms of grief.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I think it's safe to say, I am completely in love with Nick. Bless him! What a wonderful man. He made mistakes, yes, but oh wow, if every man was as good as Nick Anderson, what an amazing place the world would be.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The opposite of love isn't hate, it's indifference. And you couldn't be indifferent to him if your life depended on it."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The book ends with the perfect perfect epilogue. I don't need to say any more than that, it's just perfect.<br><br>This was a 5+ star read for me. I'm going to go now and look into buying it in paperback because I'm going to force it upon anyone who will give me the time of day. I know a lot of my GR friends have already read it but a lot still have it on their TBR list... if that's you, bump it up and make a priority. If you haven't marked this as 'to read', I strongly recommend that you do. It's honestly amazing and so beautiful and it's certainly one that will sit with me for a long long time to come.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>A sweet gum tree is the chameleon of wood, it's corky exterior hiding it's inner ability to imitate anything from cherry to mahogany. But it's real value, one unrealized by most people, is it's deep red heart, steady and strong.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401130i/778071._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12016354478233291392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1237362963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12925063837583511014"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 3/25/2015)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 8/1/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This will definitely be staying on my favorites shelf after this re-read! I ate this book right up the second time just like I remember doing the first! I was actually worried that I would not feel the emotions that I did the first time I read it, because I knew what was going to happen. While I didn't blubber cry (like I remember doing the first time), I did shed quite a bit of tears still! That tells me that it'</span>
  <span id="freeText12925063837583511014" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 3/25/2015)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 8/1/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This will definitely be staying on my favorites shelf after this re-read! I ate this book right up the second time just like I remember doing the first! I was actually worried that I would not feel the emotions that I did the first time I read it, because I knew what was going to happen. While I didn't blubber cry (like I remember doing the first time), I did shed quite a bit of tears still! That tells me that it's just that good! I hate doing it (because I really did love the rest of the book), but I'm going to lower my rating to 4.5 stars. I can't justify a 5 star rating with an ending that felt rushed like it did (see below).<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Alix and Nick's story. They meet officially when Alix is 8 and Nick is 10 when she goes to his father's junkyard to get a car part. They form a unlikely friendship that holds through the years but devolops into something more when they grow older. There is a tragic event that separates them, and when Nick returns ~15 years later he doesn't get the welcome home he was expecting. There are some cute moments, some sad moments, and some sweet moments...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told in Alix's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good until the end (see closure section). I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well otherwise.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they've known each other for years.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Nick. I liked him. He was loyal to a fault, but I appreciated that about him (even when I wanted to shake him a few times). <br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Alix. I liked her. I especially liked young Alix! She was strong and feisty.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate/high. I cried but I didn't need any tissues this go-round, but I definitely remember crying a lot more the first time!<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H pushes away in the past, and the h pushes away in the present. Both pursue the relationship at times.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Low. The scenes were non-descriptive and more about the emotional connection between the couple.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> No. This is a perfect example of how fade-to-black or non-descriptive sex scenes can work with a book! The connection was so strong otherwise that I didn't even miss it!<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> No mentions of any safe sex specifics.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a OW that grew up always around the H. She causes some drama for the couple.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Not between mcs <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Side characters, and the h is dating OM awhile she is secretly with (and intimate with) the H. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for about 15 years. The h was married to OM, and there is mention of her being intimate with him. The H says he went on dates but i felt like it was implied that it never went further than dates with those OW.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Alcoholic and abusive parent (H - aftermath), prostitution (side character off page), rape/murder (side character off page), attempted rape (on page), unexpected pregnancy (on page), and loss of child to SIDS (off page - through many mentions).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had pretty good closure, but I wanted more! I would call it a HEA...but it was super quick, and I wanted to experience more of that happiness after all the bad things I went through with them!<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid $0.99 for it back in 2015 on Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating by mcs<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse by mcs<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="12925063837583511014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText9834361664086313019" style="display:none">You have to read this UTTERLY MAGNINIFICENT book!! Nick and Alix's love story will compell you like no other. This is the book I have wanted to read since I can't even remenber. What I loved most about it was all the emotions it induced in me...but most of all, I could not get enough of Nick, Alix and their love...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380377035i/732222.gif" height="250" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749777.jpg" width="400" height="285" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is one of the, hands down, most beautiful books I have ever read. It is actually one of the best books I ever had the pleasure of reading <i>ever,</i>period. This book made me feel things hardly any books do. The writing was fantastic, the caracters were amazing and the story, description and development was wonderful. I completely and utterly fell in love with Nick and Alix´s love story. From the moment they met as children until the book stops, 28 years later.It grabs an hold on you and don´t let go. I was literally on the edge of my seat while I read this, with a racing heart. Even now, a few days later, I can´t stop thinking about it. I so wish the author could have given us a little more details but I devoured and savoured every word while reading, and I am satisfied how it all turned out in the end. I would really like to continue to read about these amazing caracters in a sequel. Why oh why, couldn´t it have been longer? I wish there were more books like this, it really touched my heart.<br><br>It is books like <b>THE SWEET GUM TREE</b> that is my reason for reading, because every once in a while you stumbles across pearls like this. <b>PERFECTION DEFINED</b>.<br><br>Simply <b>BREATHTAKING</b> and <b>TERRIFIC</b>. It is a must read. Go and pick it up today! Please! Be prepared for an emotional roller coaster.....<br><br>I have a new favorite author and her name is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1077176.Katherine_Allred" title="Katherine Allred" rel="nofollow noopener">Katherine Allred</a>.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i> “He always was someone. Because the core of the sweet gum tree never changes. Like Nick, the deep red wood stays true to its nature. Strong, and steady, and pure.” </i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749779.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1960760097979338791">5 Broken Hearts Stars! <br/><br/>Reread 11/19 Still a 5 star read for me! I loved this one just as much the second time around! <br/><br/><a href='http://s298.photobucket.com/user/michellehofelich/media/image.jpg1_zpsbwiqtbpu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437378745i/15579539.jpg' alt=' photo image.jpg1_zpsbwiqtbpu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Alix French was 8 years old when she went to the scrap yard with her grandfather (Judge) and met 10 year old Nick Anderson.
